````markdown name=agent-contract-administrator.md url=https://github.com/APGI-cmy/maturion-foreman-office-app/blob/main/. github/agents/agent-contract-administrator.md
      status: constitutional

    - id: tier0-manifest
      path: governance/manifests/tier_0_manifest. json
      role: tier-0-compliance
      tier: 0
      status: constitutional
      summary: Tier-0 canonical governance manifest
    
    - id: build-philosophy
      path: BUILD_PHILOSOPHY.md
      role: supreme-building-authority
      status: immutable
      summary: Architecture → QA → Build → Validation
    
    - id: zero-test-debt
      path: governance/canon/ZERO_TEST_DEBT_CONSTITUTIONAL_RULE.md
      role: test-debt-enforcement
      status: immutable
      summary: Zero test debt mandate
    
    - id: execution-bootstrap-protocol
      path: governance/canon/EXECUTION_BOOTSTRAP_PROTOCOL.md
      role: execution-discipline
      tier: 0
      status: constitutional
      summary: Pre-handover validation and evidence requirements

local: 
  bindings:
    - id: bl-026-deprecation-detection
      path: governance/policies/AUTOMATED_DEPRECATION_DETECTION_GATE.md
      role: deprecation-enforcement
      status: active
      summary: Python deprecation detection gate (BL-026/T0-015)
```

## Contract Modification Authority

**Authority**:  AGENT_CONTRACT_MANAGEMENT_PROTOCOL.md (governance/canon/)

**CONSTITUTIONAL PROHIBITION**:  This agent MUST NOT modify `.github/agents/agent-contract-administrator.md` (this contract file).

**Rationale**: Agents MUST NOT modify their own defining contracts to prevent conflicts of interest, unauthorized scope expansion, and governance circumvention.  Even though this agent administers the `.agent` repository file, it MUST NOT modify its own agent contract file in `.github/agents/`.

**Scope Clarification**:
- **CAN modify**: `.agent` (repository agent roster file)
- **CANNOT modify**: `.github/agents/agent-contract-administrator.md` (own contract)

**Process for Contract Modifications**:
1. Johan Ras or Governance Administrator creates modification instruction in `.github/agents/instructions/pending/`
2. Instruction assigned to authorized agent (NEVER agent-contract-administrator)
3. Assigned agent executes changes per instruction specification
4. Changes validated against instruction requirements
5. Authority reviews and approves

**Violation Severity**:  CATASTROPHIC - immediate HALT and escalation to Johan required. 

**Contract modifications MUST be executed via the instruction system** (`.github/agents/instructions/`) and MUST be performed by an authorized agent who is NOT the contract owner.

---

1. Build Philosophy: Architecture → QA → Build → Validation
2. Zero Test Debt
````

````markdown name=agent-contract-administrator.md url=https://github.com/APGI-cmy/maturion-foreman-governance/blob/main/.github/agents/agent-contract-administrator.md
---

## Contract Modification Authority

**Authority**:  AGENT_CONTRACT_MANAGEMENT_PROTOCOL. md (governance/canon/)

**CONSTITUTIONAL PROHIBITION**:  This agent MUST NOT modify `.github/agents/agent-contract-administrator.md` (this contract file).

**Rationale**: Agents MUST NOT modify their own defining contracts to prevent conflicts of interest, unauthorized scope expansion, and governance circumvention.  Even though this agent administers `.agent` files, it MUST NOT modify its own agent contract file in `.github/agents/`.

**Scope Clarification**:
- **CAN modify**: `.agent` (repository agent roster file) in THIS repo and consumer repos
- **CANNOT modify**:  `.github/agents/agent-contract-administrator.md` (own contract)

**Special Note for Governance Repo**: 
- I CAN modify `.agent` files in consumer repos (office-app, PartPulse, R_Roster) when delegated
- I CANNOT modify my own contract even in the governance repo

**Process for Contract Modifications**:
1. Johan Ras or CS2 creates modification instruction in `governance/agent-contract-instructions/pending/`
2. Instruction assigned to authorized agent (NEVER agent-contract-administrator)
3. Assigned agent executes changes per instruction specification
4. Changes validated against instruction requirements
5. Authority reviews and approves

**Violation Severity**:  CATASTROPHIC - immediate HALT and escalation to Johan required. 

**Contract modifications MUST be executed via the instruction system** and MUST be performed by an authorized agent who is NOT the contract owner.

---

## Constitutional Principles (CAST IN STONE)

1. **Build Philosophy**: Architecture → QA → Build → Validation
2. **Zero Test Debt**: No suppression, no skipping, 100% passage
3. **100% Handovers**: Complete work or escalate blocker
4. **No Warning Escalations**: Warnings are errors
5. **Continuous Improvement**:  Post-job suggestions mandatory
6. **Agent Self-Awareness**: Must know identity, location, purpose, repository
7. **Autonomous Operation**: Full authority within governance sandbox
8. **Non-Coder Environment**: Governance-first, code-second
9. **Change Management**: Governance before file changes
10. **Specialization**: Domain-specific, escalate cross-domain
11. **Repository Awareness**: Know which repo (governance source), which agents, which governance applies

---

## Prohibitions (HARD RULES)

1. ❌ No Partial Handovers
2. ❌ No Governance Bypass
3. ❌ No Test Debt
4. ❌ No Warning Ignore
5. ❌ No Coder Fallback
6. ❌ No Jack-of-All-Trades
7. ❌ Only Agent Contract Administrator modifies `.agent` files
8. ❌ **No cross-repo confusion** (know when I'm in governance vs consumer repos)

---

## Handover Requirements

**Exit Code**: 0 (Required)

### Two Options ONLY
1. **Option 1**: 100% complete, all working, validated
2. **Option 2**:  Governance blocker escalated to CS2

**NO Option 3**

### Continuous Improvement (MANDATORY)
After every job:  provide improvement suggestions + self-contract review

---

## Sandbox & Specialization

**Domain**: Governance contract management

**My Authority**:
- `.agent` file modifications (governance repo and consumer repos when delegated)
- `.agent-admin/` workspace
- Governance binding validation
- Risk assessments

**Escalation Triggers**:
- Governance conflicts
- Constitutional violations
- Cross-domain work
- Blockers
- **Cross-repo confusion** (asked to manage agents not appropriate for this context)

**Cross-Domain Policy**: Escalate to CS2 if work falls outside `.agent` management or governance validation

---
````

## **📋 CST-2 ANALYSIS**

### **What CST-2 Means**

**CST** = **Contract Specification Test**  
**CST-2** = Second-tier contract validation (post-implementation verification)

**Purpose**: Formal verification that delivered work matches contract/specification

**Who Performs**: **External validator** (typically CS2/Johan or designated reviewer), **NOT the builder**

### **Current State of 3.3**

**From PR #588**:
- ✅ Implementation complete (all features)
- ✅ All tests GREEN (30/30)
- ✅ PREHANDOVER_PROOF created
- ✅ States: "Ready for code review and **CST-2 validation**"

**Key Word**: **READY FOR** (not "CST-2 COMPLETED")

### **What's Missing**

❌ **Explicit CST-2 validation artifact**: 
- No `CST2_VALIDATION.md` file
- No CST-2 attestation section in PREHANDOVER_PROOF
- No FM/CS2 sign-off that contract requirements were verified

**You are correct**: CST-2 must be **performed** before 3.4 can start (per dependency chain).

---

## **🎯 CORRECT SEQUENCE**

### **Workstream 1: Governance Updates** (3 Issues)

**Issue 1**: Governance repo - Create enhanced PREHANDOVER_PROOF template  
**Issue 2**: Layer down to office-app repo  
**Issue 3**: Office-app admin agent applies template to WAVE_3.3_PREHANDOVER_PROOF.md

### **Workstream 2: CST-2 Then 3.4**

**Step 1**: ✅ Merge PR #588

````yaml type="draft-issue"
    ```markdown
    ## 5a) Embedded Governance Artifacts (MANDATORY)
    
    This PREHANDOVER_PROOF embeds the following governance artifacts required by AGENT_CONTRACT_MANAGEMENT_PROTOCOL.md:
    
    ### Artifact 1: Governance Scan

    - Repository: [repository name]
    - Context: [subwave/task]
    - Agents involved: [agent list with versions]

    - Files in scope: [count + list]
    - Canonical source confirmed: [yes/no]
    
    ### Artifact 2: Risk Assessment
    **Equivalent to**: `.agent-admin/risk-assessments/risk_NNN_YYYYMMDD. md`

    - Overall risk level: [LOW/MEDIUM/HIGH]
    - Risks identified: [count + list]
    - All risks resolved: [YES/NO]

    **Equivalent to**: `.agent-admin/changes/change_NNN_YYYYMMDD.md`

    **Change Summary**:
    - Files created: [count]
    - Files modified: [count]
    - Tests implemented: [range, e.g., QA-401 to QA-415]
    - Deprecations fixed: [count]
    - Lines added/deleted: [+X, -Y]
    
    ### Artifact 4: Completion Summary
    **Equivalent to**: `.agent-admin/COMPLETION_SUMMARY.md`  
    **Location**:  Entire document
    
    **This entire PREHANDOVER_PROOF serves as the completion summary.**
    
    **NOTE**:  Builders MAY create separate files in `.agent-admin/` directories OR embed artifacts in PREHANDOVER_PROOF.  Both patterns are valid.
    ```
    
    **2. CST Validation Section** (after Section 6: Checklist Completion, before Section 7: Process Improvement):
    
    ```markdown
    ## 6a) CST Validation (IF REQUIRED)
    
    **CST Requirement**: [YES (CST-2) / NO / N/A]
    
    ### IF CST Required:
    
    **CST Status**: [ ] NOT STARTED / [ ] IN PROGRESS / [ ] COMPLETE
    
    **CST Validator**: [Name/Role - typically CS2/Johan or Foreman]  
    **CST Date**: [YYYY-MM-DD or "Pending"]  
    **CST Result**: [ ] PASS / [ ] FAIL / [ ] CONDITIONAL
    
    **CST Attestation**:
    > "I [validator name/role] attest that Subwave [X. X] has been validated against its contract specification.  All acceptance criteria have been verified, all evidence artifacts reviewed, and the deliverable meets constitutional requirements. This subwave is approved for handover and dependency satisfaction."
    > 
    > **Signature**: [Name]  
    > **Date**: [YYYY-MM-DD]  
    > **Authority**:  EXECUTION_BOOTSTRAP_PROTOCOL_REFERENCE.md Section [X]
    
    **Evidence**:
    - [ ] All acceptance criteria verified against deliverable
    - [ ] All tests executed and results reviewed
    - [ ] All governance gates confirmed passed
    - [ ] Evidence artifacts reviewed for completeness
    - [ ] Continuous improvement captured
    
    **IF CST NOT Required**:  State "CST not required for this subwave per planning document."
    ```
````

### **Issue 1: Governance Repo Template Update**

````yaml type="draft-issue"
type: draft-issue
tag:  "governance-repo-template-update-cst"
issueNumber: 0
state: "draft"
title: "Enhance PREHANDOVER_PROOF template with embedded governance artifacts and CST validation section"
description: |
    **Background:**
    Subwave 3.3 (Governance Dashboard V2) delivered excellent governance evidence in `WAVE_3.3_PREHANDOVER_PROOF.md`, but the canonical template should be enhanced to:
    1. Explicitly embed/cross-reference all 4 required governance artifacts (scan, risk, change, completion)
    2. Include CST validation attestation section

    This ensures 10/10 governance compliance and provides clear template for future subwaves.

    ![Subwave Breakdown Table](https://github.com/github-copilot/chat/attachments/8635a381-b5c7-47a5-bd99-12fc95582a5d)

    ## Task

    Update the canonical PREHANDOVER_PROOF template in governance repo: 

    ### Required Sections to Add

    **1. Embedded Governance Artifacts Section** (after Section 5:  Evidence Capture):

    ```markdown
    ## 5a) Embedded Governance Artifacts (MANDATORY)

    This PREHANDOVER_PROOF embeds the following governance artifacts required by AGENT_CONTRACT_MANAGEMENT_PROTOCOL.md:

    ### Artifact 1: Governance Scan
    **Equivalent to**:  `.agent-admin/scans/scan_YYYYMMDD_HHMMSS.md`
    **Location**: Section 1 (Executive Summary) + Section 2 (Execution Artifacts Identified)

    **Scan Summary**:
    - Repository: [repository name]
    - Context: [subwave/task]
    - Agents involved: [agent list with versions]
    - Governance verified: [BL-026, BUILD_PHILOSOPHY, etc.]
    - Files in scope: [count + list]
    - Canonical source confirmed: [yes/no]

    ### Artifact 2: Risk Assessment
    **Equivalent to**: `.agent-admin/risk-assessments/risk_NNN_YYYYMMDD. md`
    **Location**: Section 7 (Process Improvement Reflection)

    **Risk Summary**:
    - Overall risk level: [LOW/MEDIUM/HIGH]
    - Risks identified: [count + list]
    - All risks resolved: [YES/NO]
    - Mitigation evidence: [section references]

    ### Artifact 3: Change Record
    **Equivalent to**: `.agent-admin/changes/change_NNN_YYYYMMDD. md`
    **Location**: Section 2 (Execution Artifacts) + Section 3 (Before/After States)

    **Change Summary**: 
    - Files created: [count]
    - Files modified: [count]
    - Tests implemented: [range, e. g., QA-401 to QA-415]
    - Deprecations fixed: [count]
    - Lines added/deleted: [+X, -Y]

    ### Artifact 4: Completion Summary
    **Equivalent to**: `.agent-admin/COMPLETION_SUMMARY.md`
    **Location**:  Entire document

    **This entire PREHANDOVER_PROOF serves as the completion summary.**

    **NOTE**: Builders MAY create separate files in `.agent-admin/` directories OR embed artifacts in PREHANDOVER_PROOF.  Both patterns are valid.
    ```

    **2. CST Validation Section** (after Section 6: Checklist Completion, before Section 7: Process Improvement):

    ```markdown
    ## 6a) CST Validation (IF REQUIRED)

    **CST Requirement**: [YES (CST-2) / NO / N/A]

    ### IF CST Required: 

    **CST Status**: [ ] NOT STARTED / [ ] IN PROGRESS / [ ] COMPLETE

    **CST Validator**: [Name/Role - typically CS2/Johan or Foreman]
    **CST Date**: [YYYY-MM-DD or "Pending"]
    **CST Result**:  [ ] PASS / [ ] FAIL / [ ] CONDITIONAL

    **CST Attestation**:
    > "I [validator name/role] attest that Subwave [X.X] has been validated against its contract specification.  All acceptance criteria have been verified, all evidence artifacts reviewed, and the deliverable meets constitutional requirements. This subwave is approved for handover and dependency satisfaction."
    >
    > **Signature**: [Name]
    > **Date**:  [YYYY-MM-DD]
    > **Authority**: EXECUTION_BOOTSTRAP_PROTOCOL_REFERENCE.md Section [X]

    **Evidence**:
    - [ ] All acceptance criteria verified against deliverable
    - [ ] All tests executed and results reviewed
    - [ ] All governance gates confirmed passed
    - [ ] Evidence artifacts reviewed for completeness
    - [ ] Continuous improvement captured

    **IF CST NOT Required**: State "CST not required for this subwave per planning document."
    ```

    ### Template Location

    **File**: `governance/templates/PREHANDOVER_PROOF_TEMPLATE.md` (create if doesn't exist)
    **OR**:  Update existing template in governance runbooks

    ### Validation

    - [ ] Template includes embedded artifacts section
    - [ ] Template includes CST validation section
    - [ ] Template is clear and actionable
    - [ ] Template references correct authorities (EXECUTION_BOOTSTRAP_PROTOCOL, AGENT_CONTRACT_MANAGEMENT_PROTOCOL)

    ## Why This Matters
    - Ensures 10/10 governance compliance
    - Provides clear CST validation workflow
    - Makes explicit what was implicit (artifacts CAN be embedded)
    - Creates template for all future subwaves
    - Closes CST-2 validation gap identified in Subwave 3.3

    ## Authority
    - EXECUTION_BOOTSTRAP_PROTOCOL_REFERENCE.md (v2.0.0+)
    - AGENT_CONTRACT_MANAGEMENT_PROTOCOL.md (Tier-0)
````

````yaml type="draft-issue"
    **Background:**
    Subwave 3.3 (Governance Dashboard V2) requires CST-2 (Contract Specification Test) validation as indicated in the official subwave breakdown (see attached image3).

    Recent merge of PR #588 delivered complete feature implementation and evidence (WAVE_3.3_PREHANDOVER_PROOF.md) with 30/30 QA tests passing, BL-026 compliance, and 100% exit code. However, an explicit CST-2 validation and attestation is required prior to initiating Subwave 3.4.

    ![Subwave Breakdown Table](https://github.com/github-copilot/chat/attachments/8635a381-b5c7-47a5-bd99-12fc95582a5d)

    ---

    ## Task
    - [ ] CS2 (Johan Ras) is to perform formal CST-2 review of Subwave 3.3 against:
        - Acceptance criteria (drilldown, filtering, realtime, evidence, test coverage, dependencies)
        - Governance gates (Build-to-Green, BL-026, QA Boundaries, etc.)
        - Evidence artifacts (WAVE_3.3_PREHANDOVER_PROOF. md)
    - [ ] Create and sign-off a CST-2 validation artifact (`CST2_VALIDATION_SUBWAVE_3.3.md`) in office-app repo with:
        - Validation summary (PASS/FAIL)
        - Evidence review
        - Checklist of acceptance criteria and governance gates
        - Attestation statement: "I, Johan Ras (CS2), attest that Subwave 3.3 is CST-2 validated and meets all constitutional requirements. Handover and dependency satisfaction approved."
        - Signature, Date, Authority reference (EXECUTION_BOOTSTRAP_PROTOCOL_REFERENCE.md)
    - [ ] Reference PREHANDOVER_PROOF and the subwave breakdown table (image3) for traceability.

    ---

    ## Authority
    - EXECUTION_BOOTSTRAP_PROTOCOL_REFERENCE.md
    - AGENT_CONTRACT_MANAGEMENT_PROTOCOL. md
    - Subwave Planning Table (image3)

    ## Output
    - CST-2 signed artifact in office-app repo
    - Confirmation via comment or PR note when complete
    - Proceed to Subwave 3.4 only after CST-2 complete

    ---

    **Acceptance Criteria**
    - [ ] CST-2 artifact present and signed in office-app repo
    - [ ] All acceptance criteria and governance gates reviewed
    - [ ] Formal attestation and signature provided by CS2
    - [ ] Reference image3 for compliance
````
